                at&nbsp;<a href="/maps-platform/terms/maps-service-terms" class="cws-link" track-name="https//cloudgooglecom/maps-platform/terms/maps-service-terms/" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/maps-service-terms/" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/maps-service-terms/</a>.
              </p>
              <p>"<em>Maps Technical Support Services</em>" means the technical
                support service provided by Google to Customer under the
                then-current Maps Technical Support Services Guidelines.</p>
              <p>"<em>Maps Technical Support Services Guidelines</em>" means the
                then-current technical support service guidelines described
                at&nbsp;<a href="/maps-platform/terms/tssg" class="cws-link" track-name="https//cloudgooglecom/maps-platform/terms/tssg/" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/tssg/" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/tssg/</a>.
              </p>
              <p>"<em>Personal Data</em>" has the meaning given to it in: (a)
                Regulation (EU) 2016/679 of the European Parliament and of the
                Council of 27 April 2016 on the protection of natural persons
                with regard to the processing of personal data and on the free
                movement of such data, and repealing Directive 95/46/EC (â€œEU
                GDPRâ€); or (b) the EU GDPR as amended and incorporated into UK
                law under the UK European Union (Withdrawal) Act 2018 (â€œUK
                GDPRâ€), if in force, as applicable.</p>
              <p>"<em>Notification Email Address</em>" means the email
                address(es) designated by Customer in the Admin Console.</p>
              <p>"<em>Price</em>" means the then-current applicable price(s)
                stated
                at&nbsp;<a href="/maps-platform/pricing/sheet" class="cws-link" track-name="https//cloudgooglecom/maps-platform/pricing/sheet/" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/maps-platform/pricing/sheet/" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/pricing/sheet/</a>.
              </p>
              <p>"<em>Prohibited Territory</em>" means the countries listed
                at&nbsp;<a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/maps-prohibited-territories/&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1524619731812000" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="https//cloudgooglecom/maps-platform/terms/maps-prohibited-territories/" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="www.google.com/url" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/maps-prohibited-territories/</a>.
              </p>
              <p>"<em>Project</em>"&nbsp;means a Customer-selected grouping of
                Google Maps Core Services resources for a particular Customer
                Application.</p>
              <p>"<em>Reseller</em>"&nbsp;means, if applicable, the authorized
                unaffiliated third-party reseller that sells or supplies the
                Services to Customer.</p>
              <p>"<em>Reseller Agreement</em>"&nbsp;means, if applicable, a
                separate, independent agreement between Customer and Reseller
                regarding the Services.</p>
              <p>"<em>Reseller Order Form</em>"&nbsp;means an order form entered
                into by Reseller and Customer, subject to the Reseller
                Agreement.</p>
              <p>"<em>Services</em>" and "<em>Google Maps Core
                  Services</em>"&nbsp;means the services described
                at&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/maps-services" class="cws-link" track-name="https//cloudgooglecom/maps-platform/terms/maps-services/" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/maps-services" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/maps-services/</a>.
                The Services include the Google Maps Content and the Software.
              </p>
              <p>"<em>Significant Backwards Incompatible Change</em>"&nbsp;means a material
                discontinuance or material backwards incompatible change to the Google
                Maps Core Services described at&nbsp;
                <a href="https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/maps-services/" class="cws-link">https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/maps-services/</a>.
                <a href="https://developers.google.com/maps/software-support" class="cws-link" target="_blank">Freezing software support</a> does not constitute a Significant Backwards Incompatible Change.
              </p>
              <p>"<em>SLA</em>"&nbsp;or "<em>Service&nbsp;Level
                  Agreement</em>"&nbsp;means each of the then-current service
                level agreements
                at:&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/sla" class="cws-link" track-name="https//cloudgooglecom/maps-platform/terms/sla/" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/sla" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/sla/</a>.
              </p>
              <p>"<em>Software</em>" means any downloadable tools, software
                development kits, or other computer software provided by Google
                for use as part of the Services, including updates.</p>
              <p>"<em>Suspend</em>" or "<em>Suspension</em>&nbsp;" means
                disabling access to or use of the Services or components of the
                Services.</p>
              <p>"<em>Taxes</em>" means any duties, customs fees, or
                government-imposed taxes associated with the purchase of the
                Services, including any related penalties or interest, except
                for taxes based on Googleâ€™s net income, net worth, asset value,
                property value, or employment.</p>
              <p>"<em>Term</em>" has the meaning stated in
                Section&nbsp;11.1&nbsp;of the Agreement.</p>
              <p>â€œ<em>Terms URL</em>â€ means the following URL set forth
                here:&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms" class="cws-link" track-name="https//cloudgooglecom/maps-platform/terms/" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://cloud.google.com/maps-platform/terms/</a>.
              </p>
              <p>"<em>Third-Party Legal Proceeding</em>" means any formal legal
                proceeding filed by an unaffiliated third party before a court
                or government tribunal (including any appellate proceeding).</p>
              <p>"<em>Trademark Guidelines</em>"&nbsp;means (a) Googleâ€™s Brand
                Terms and Conditions, located
                at:&nbsp;<a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.google.com/permissions/trademark/brand-terms.html&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1524619731816000" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="https//wwwgooglecom/permissions/trademark/brand-termshtml" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="www.google.com/url" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://www.google.com/permissions/trademark/brand-terms.html</a>&nbsp;and
                (b) the â€œUse of Trademarksâ€ section of the â€œUsing Google Maps,
                Google Earth and Street Viewâ€ permissions page
                at&nbsp;<a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.google.com/permissions/geoguidelines.html%23geotrademark&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1524619731817000" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="https//wwwgooglecom/permissions/geoguidelineshtmlgeotrademark" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="www.google.com/url" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://www.google.com/permissions/geoguidelines.html#geotrademark</a>&nbsp;policy.
              </p>
              <p>â€œ<em>URL Terms</em>â€ means the following, which will control in
                the following order if there is a conflict:</p>
              <p>(a) the Maps Service Specific Terms;</p>
              <p>(b) the SLA;</p>
              <p>(c) the AUP;</p>
              <p>(d) the Maps Technical Support Services Guidelines;</p>
              <p>(e) the Legal Notices for Google Maps/Google Earth and Google
                Maps/Google Earth APIs
                at&nbsp;<a href="https://www.google.com/help/legalnotices_maps.html" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="https//wwwgooglecom/help/legalnotices_mapshtml" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="www.google.com/help/legalnotices_maps.html" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://www.google.com/help/legalnotices_maps.html</a>;
                and</p>
              <p>(f) the Google Maps/Google Earth Additional Terms of Service
                at&nbsp;<a href="https://maps.google.com/help/terms_maps.html" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="https//mapsgooglecom/help/terms_mapshtml" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="maps.google.com/help/terms_maps.html" track-metadata-module="text blocks">https://maps.google.com/help/terms_maps.html</a>.
              </p>
              <p><strong>22.&nbsp;Regional Terms.</strong></p>
              <p>Customer agrees to the following modifications to the Agreement
                if Customer orders Services from the applicable Google entity as
                described below:</p>
              <div
                class="cloud-table-wrapper devsite-table-wrapper cloud-table-wrapper--alternate">
                <table class="cloud-table">
                  <tbody>
                    <tr>
                      <td colspan="2"><strong>Asia Pacific - Indonesia</strong>
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                      <td>PT Google Cloud Indonesia</td>
                      <td>
                        <p>1.&nbsp;The following is added as Section 11.6
                          (Termination Waiver):</p>
                        <p>11.6&nbsp;<em>Termination Waiver</em>. The parties
                          agree to waive any provisions under any applicable
                          laws to the extent that a court decision or order is
                          required for the termination of this Agreement.</p>
                        <p>2.&nbsp;Section 19.11 (Governing Law) is deleted and
                          replaced with the following:</p>
                        <p>19.11&nbsp;<em>Governing Law</em>.</p>
                        <p>(a)&nbsp;The parties will try in good faith to settle
                          any dispute within 30 days after the dispute arises.
                          If the dispute is not resolved within 30 days, it must
                          be resolved by arbitration by the American Arbitration
                          Associationâ€™s International Centre for Dispute
                          Resolution in accordance with its Expedited Commercial
                          Rules in force as of the date of the Agreement
                          ("Rules").</p>
                        <p>(b)&nbsp;The parties will mutually select one
                          arbitrator. The arbitration will be conducted in
                          English in Santa Clara County, California, USA.</p>
                        <p>(c)&nbsp;Either party may apply to any competent
                          court for injunctive relief necessary to protect its
                          rights pending resolution of the arbitration. The
                          arbitrator may order equitable or injunctive relief
                          consistent with the remedies and limitations in the
                          Agreement.</p>
                        <p>(d)&nbsp;Subject to the confidentiality requirements
                          in Section 19.11(f), either party may petition any
                          competent court to issue any order necessary to
                          protect that partyâ€™s rights or property; this petition
                          will not be considered a violation or waiver of this
                          governing law and arbitration section and will not
                          affect the arbitratorâ€™s powers, including the power to
                          review the judicial decision. The parties stipulate
                          that the courts of Santa Clara County, California,
                          USA, are competent to grant any order under this
                          Section 19.11(d).</p>
                        <p>(e)&nbsp;The arbitral award will be final and binding
                          on the parties and its execution may be presented in
                          any competent court, including any court with
                          jurisdiction over either party or any of its property.
                        </p>
                        <p>(f)&nbsp;Any arbitration proceeding conducted in
                          accordance with this Section will be considered
                          Confidential Information under the Agreementâ€™s
                          confidentiality section, including (i) the existence
                          of, (ii) any information disclosed during, and (iii)
                          any oral communications or documents related to the
                          arbitration proceedings. The parties may also disclose
                          the information described in this Section 19.11(f) to
                          a competent court as may be necessary to file any
                          order under Section 19.11(d) or execute any arbitral
                          decision, but the parties must request that those
                          judicial proceedings be conducted in camera (in
                          private).</p>
                        <p>(g)&nbsp;The parties will pay the arbitratorâ€™s fees,
                          the arbitratorâ€™s appointed expertsâ€™ fees and expenses,
                          and the arbitration centerâ€™s administrative expenses
                          in accordance with the Rules. In its final decision,
                          the arbitrator will determine the non-prevailing
                          partyâ€™s obligation to reimburse the amount paid in
                          advance by the prevailing party for these fees.</p>
                        <p>(h)&nbsp;Each party will bear its own lawyersâ€™ and
                          expertsâ€™ fees and expenses, regardless of the
                          arbitratorâ€™s final decision regarding the Dispute.</p>
                        <p>(i)&nbsp;The parties agree that a decision of the
                          arbitrators need not to be made within any specific
                          time period.</p>
                        <p>3.&nbsp;Section 19.15 (Conflicting Languages) is
                          deleted and replaced with the following:</p>
                        <p>19.15&nbsp;<em>Conflicting Languages</em>.&nbsp;This
                          Agreement is made in the Indonesian and the English
                          language, and both versions are equally authentic. In
                          the event of any inconsistency or different
                          interpretation between the Indonesian version and the
                          English version, the parties agree to amend the
                          Indonesian version to make the relevant part of the
                          Indonesian version consistent with the relevant part
                          of the English version.</p>
                      </td>
